---

### Summary of `README.md`

The `README.md` is the main entrypoint for the **Consoul** project, an AIpowered terminal assistant.

**Key points**

| Section | What it covers |
|---------|----------------|
| **Intro** | Describes Consoul as a TUI/CLI + SDK that lets you chat with Claude, GPT4, Gemini, or local models. |
| **Quick Start** | Installation via `pip install consoul`, setting API keys, launching the TUI (`consoul`) or using the SDK (`Consoul`). |
| **Features** |  Beautiful TUI (Textual) with multiturn chat, streaming, file attachments, themes.<br> Multiprovider support (Claude, OpenAI, Gemini, Ollama, LlamaCpp).<br> Builtin AI tools: file editing, code search, image analysis, bash execution, web search. |
| **CLI & SDK** | Quick examples of using the command line (`consoul chat`, `consoul ask`) and embedding in Python. |
| **Documentation** | Links to the full docs, configuration guide, and more. |
| **Configuration** | Example `~/.consoul/config.yaml` showing profiles, models, tool permissions, conversation settings. |
| **Security** | Overview of permission policies, approval workflows, audit logging, command validation. |
| **Contribution** | Notes that contributions are welcome, reference `CONTRIBUTING.md`. |
| **License** | MIT License. |
| **Built With** | Textual, LangChain, Anthropic, OpenAI, Google AI. |

The README functions as a quickstart guide, feature highlight, and reference for users and contributors., has_tool_calls_in_message=[], full_response_len=1883, cancelled=False
